<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">📚 VIT-Papers Repository</h1><a id="user-content--vit-papers-repository" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 📚 VIT-Papers Repository" href="#-vit-papers-repository"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🏫 The Ultimate Collection of VIT B.Tech Engineering Previous Year Question Papers</h3><a id="user-content--the-ultimate-collection-of-vit-btech-engineering-previous-year-question-papers" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🏫 The Ultimate Collection of VIT B.Tech Engineering Previous Year Question Papers" href="#-the-ultimate-collection-of-vit-btech-engineering-previous-year-question-papers"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Welcome to <strong>VIT-Papers</strong>, your go-to resource for <strong>650+ previous year question papers</strong>
across <strong>150+ engineering courses</strong> at VIT, covering campuses in <strong>Vellore, Chennai, Bhopal, and AP</strong>.
This repository brings together essential exam preparation materials for <strong>Continuous Assessment Tests (CATs)</strong>
and <strong>Final Assessment Tests (FATs)</strong>, helping you succeed in your academic journey.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">📂 Repository Structure</h2><a id="user-content--repository-structure" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 📂 Repository Structure" href="#-repository-structure"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Each course folder is neatly organized by name, making it easy for you to find what you
need. Here are some of the domains covered:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Computer Science and Engineering (CSE)</strong></li>
<li><strong>Electronics and Communication Engineering (ECE)</strong></li>
<li><strong>Mechanical Engineering</strong></li>
<li><strong>Chemical Engineering</strong></li>
<li><strong>Electrical and Electronics Engineering (EEE)</strong></li>
<li><strong>Civil Engineering</strong></li>
<li><strong>Biotechnology</strong></li>
<li><strong>Automobile Engineering</strong></li>
<li><strong>Information Technology (IT)</strong></li>
<li><strong>Biomedical Engineering</strong></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">With this repository, you have a comprehensive study resource at your fingertips, covering
a wide array of engineering domains to support your B.Tech coursework and exams.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">📖 How to Use</h2><a id="user-content--how-to-use" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 📖 How to Use" href="#-how-to-use"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Find Your Course</strong>: Browse the folders to locate your course by name.</li>
<li><strong>Access Papers</strong>: Open the course folder to view and download question papers.</li>
<li><strong>Prepare &amp; Succeed</strong>: Practice with these question papers to get familiar with</li>
<li>exam patterns and strengthen your understanding!</li>
</ol>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="warning">⚠️</g-emoji> Disclaimer</h2><a id="user-content-️-disclaimer" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: ⚠️ Disclaimer" href="#️-disclaimer"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

Materials are shared solely to help students prepare and excel in their exams.</p>
